pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:0.4
Pali: 3. Ekagāmantaragamanasikkhāpada 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.1
Pali: Tena samayena buddho bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.2
Pali: Tena kho pana samayena bhaddāya kāpilāniyā antevāsinī bhikkhunī bhikkhunīhi saddhiṁ bhaṇḍitvā gāmakaṁ ñātikulaṁ agamāsi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.3
Pali: Bhaddā kāpilānī taṁ bhikkhuniṁ apassantī bhikkhuniyo pucchi—“kahaṁ itthannāmā, na dissatī”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.4
Pali: “Bhikkhunīhi saddhiṁ, ayye, bhaṇḍitvā na dissatī”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.5
Pali: “Ammā, amukasmiṁ gāmake etissā ñātikulaṁ. Tattha gantvā vicinathā”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.6
Pali: Bhikkhuniyo tattha gantvā taṁ bhikkhuniṁ passitvā etadavocuṁ—“kissa tvaṁ, ayye, ekikā āgatā, kaccisi appadhaṁsitā”ti? 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.7
Pali: “Appadhaṁsitāmhi, ayye”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.8
Pali: Yā tā bhikkhuniyo appicchā …pe… tā ujjhāyanti khiyyanti vipācenti—

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.9
Pali: “kathañhi nāma bhikkhunī ekā gāmantaraṁ gacchissatī”ti …pe… 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.10
Pali: “saccaṁ kira, bhikkhave, bhikkhunī ekā gāmantaraṁ gacchatī”ti? 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.11
Pali: “Saccaṁ, bhagavā”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.12
Pali: Vigarahi buddho bhagavā …pe… 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.13
Pali: kathañhi nāma, bhikkhave, bhikkhunī ekā gāmantaraṁ gacchissati. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.14
Pali: Netaṁ, bhikkhave, appasannānaṁ vā pasādāya …pe… 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.15
Pali: evañca pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhuniyo imaṁ sikkhāpadaṁ uddisantu—

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.16.1
Pali: “Yā pana bhikkhunī ekā gāmantaraṁ gaccheyya, ayampi bhikkhunī paṭhamāpattikaṁ dhammaṁ āpannā nissāraṇīyaṁ saṅghādisesan”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:1.17
Pali: Evañcidaṁ bhagavatā bhikkhunīnaṁ sikkhāpadaṁ paññattaṁ hoti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.1
Pali: Tena kho pana samayena dve bhikkhuniyo sāketā sāvatthiṁ addhānamaggappaṭipannā honti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.2
Pali: Antarāmagge nadī taritabbā hoti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.3
Pali: Atha kho tā bhikkhuniyo nāvike upasaṅkamitvā etadavocuṁ—“sādhu no, āvuso, tārethā”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.4
Pali: “Nāyye, sakkā ubho sakiṁ tāretun”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.5
Pali: Eko ekaṁ uttāresi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.6
Pali: Uttiṇṇo uttiṇṇaṁ dūsesi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.7
Pali: Anuttiṇṇo anuttiṇṇaṁ dūsesi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.8
Pali: Tā pacchā samāgantvā pucchiṁsu—

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.9
Pali: “kaccisi, ayye, appadhaṁsitā”ti? 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.10
Pali: “Padhaṁsitāmhi, ayye. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.11
Pali: Tvaṁ pana, ayye, appadhaṁsitā”ti? 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.12
Pali: “Padhaṁsitāmhi, ayye”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.13
Pali: Atha kho tā bhikkhuniyo sāvatthiṁ gantvā bhikkhunīnaṁ etamatthaṁ ārocesuṁ. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.14
Pali: Yā tā bhikkhuniyo appicchā …pe… tā ujjhāyanti khiyyanti vipācenti—

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.15
Pali: “kathañhi nāma bhikkhunī ekā nadīpāraṁ gacchissatī”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.16
Pali: Atha kho tā bhikkhuniyo bhikkhūnaṁ etamatthaṁ ārocesuṁ. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.17
Pali: Bhikkhū bhagavato etamatthaṁ ārocesuṁ …pe… 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.18
Pali: “saccaṁ kira, bhikkhave, bhikkhunī ekā nadīpāraṁ gacchatī”ti? 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.19
Pali: “Saccaṁ, bhagavā”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.20
Pali: Vigarahi buddho bhagavā …pe… 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.21
Pali: kathañhi nāma, bhikkhave, bhikkhunī ekā nadīpāraṁ gacchissati. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.22
Pali: Netaṁ, bhikkhave, appasannānaṁ vā pasādāya …pe… 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.23
Pali: evañca pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhuniyo imaṁ sikkhāpadaṁ uddisantu—

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.24.1
Pali: “Yā pana bhikkhunī ekā vā gāmantaraṁ gaccheyya, ekā vā nadīpāraṁ gaccheyya, ayampi bhikkhunī paṭhamāpattikaṁ dhammaṁ āpannā nissāraṇīyaṁ saṅghādisesan”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:2.25
Pali: Evañcidaṁ bhagavatā bhikkhunīnaṁ sikkhāpadaṁ paññattaṁ hoti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.1
Pali: Tena kho pana samayena sambahulā bhikkhuniyo kosalesu janapade sāvatthiṁ gacchantā sāyaṁ aññataraṁ gāmaṁ upagacchiṁsu. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.2
Pali: Tattha aññatarā bhikkhunī abhirūpā hoti dassanīyā pāsādikā. Aññataro puriso tassā bhikkhuniyā saha dassanena paṭibaddhacitto hoti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.3
Pali: Atha kho so puriso tāsaṁ bhikkhunīnaṁ seyyaṁ paññapento tassā bhikkhuniyā seyyaṁ ekamantaṁ paññāpesi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.4
Pali: Atha kho sā bhikkhunī sallakkhetvā—“pariyuṭṭhito ayaṁ puriso; sace rattiṁ āgacchissati, vissaro me bhavissatī”ti, 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.5
Pali: bhikkhuniyo anāpucchā aññataraṁ kulaṁ gantvā seyyaṁ kappesi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.6
Pali: Atha kho so puriso rattiṁ āgantvā taṁ bhikkhuniṁ gavesanto bhikkhuniyo ghaṭṭesi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.7
Pali: Bhikkhuniyo taṁ bhikkhuniṁ apassantiyo evamāhaṁsu—“nissaṁsayaṁ kho sā bhikkhunī purisena saddhiṁ nikkhantā”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.8
Pali: Atha kho sā bhikkhunī tassā rattiyā accayena yena tā bhikkhuniyo tenupasaṅkami. Bhikkhuniyo taṁ bhikkhuniṁ etadavocuṁ—“kissa tvaṁ, ayye, purisena saddhiṁ nikkhantā”ti? 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.9
Pali: “Nāhaṁ, ayye, purisena saddhiṁ nikkhantā”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.10
Pali: Bhikkhunīnaṁ etamatthaṁ ārocesi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.11
Pali: Yā tā bhikkhuniyo appicchā …pe… tā ujjhāyanti khiyyanti vipācenti—

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.12
Pali: “kathañhi nāma bhikkhunī ekā rattiṁ vippavasissatī”ti …pe… 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.13
Pali: “saccaṁ kira, bhikkhave, bhikkhunī ekā rattiṁ vippavasatī”ti? 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.14
Pali: “Saccaṁ, bhagavā”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.15
Pali: Vigarahi buddho bhagavā …pe… 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.16
Pali: kathañhi nāma, bhikkhave, bhikkhunī ekā rattiṁ vippavasissati. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.17
Pali: Netaṁ, bhikkhave, appasannānaṁ vā pasādāya …pe… 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.18
Pali: evañca pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhuniyo imaṁ sikkhāpadaṁ uddisantu—

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.19.1
Pali: “Yā pana bhikkhunī ekā vā gāmantaraṁ gaccheyya, ekā vā nadīpāraṁ gaccheyya, ekā vā rattiṁ vippavaseyya, ayampi bhikkhunī paṭhamāpattikaṁ dhammaṁ āpannā nissāraṇīyaṁ saṅghādisesan”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:3.20
Pali: Evañcidaṁ bhagavatā bhikkhunīnaṁ sikkhāpadaṁ paññattaṁ hoti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:4.1

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:4.2
Pali: Tattha aññatarā bhikkhunī vaccena pīḷitā ekikā ohīyitvā pacchā agamāsi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:4.3
Pali: Manussā taṁ bhikkhuniṁ passitvā dūsesuṁ. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:4.4

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:4.5
Pali: “Padhaṁsitāmhi, ayye”ti.

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:4.8

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss3:4.9
Pali: “Saccaṁ, bhagavā”ti.

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.1
Pali: Tena samayena buddho bhagavā sāvatthiyaṁ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.2
Pali: Tena kho pana samayena caṇḍakāḷī bhikkhunī bhaṇḍanakārikā hoti kalahakārikā vivādakārikā bhassakārikā saṅghe adhikaraṇakārikā. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.3
Pali: Thullanandā bhikkhunī tassā kamme karīyamāne paṭikkosati. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.4
Pali: Tena kho pana samayena thullanandā bhikkhunī gāmakaṁ agamāsi kenacideva karaṇīyena. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.5

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.6

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.7
Pali: Thullanandā bhikkhunī gāmake taṁ karaṇīyaṁ tīretvā punadeva sāvatthiṁ paccāgacchi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.8
Pali: Caṇḍakāḷī bhikkhunī thullanandāya bhikkhuniyā āgacchantiyā neva āsanaṁ paññapesi na pādodakaṁ pādapīṭhaṁ pādakaṭhalikaṁ upanikkhipi na paccuggantvā pattacīvaraṁ paṭiggahesi na pānīyena āpucchi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.9

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.10
Pali: “kissa tvaṁ, ayye, mayi āgacchantiyā neva āsanaṁ paññapesi na pādodakaṁ pādapīṭhaṁ pādakaṭhalikaṁ upanikkhipi na paccuggantvā pattacīvaraṁ paṭiggahesi na pānīyena āpucchī”ti? 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.11
Pali: “Evañhetaṁ, ayye, hoti yathā taṁ anāthāyā”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.12

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.15
Pali: Thullanandā bhikkhunī—

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss4:1.16

Pali: Sutvā na vadanti, āpatti dukkaṭassa.

Pali: Sā bhikkhunī saṅghamajjhampi ākaḍḍhitvā vattabbā—

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.25
Pali: “māyye, kupitā anattamanā evaṁ avaca—

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.26
Pali: ‘buddhaṁ paccācikkhāmi …pe… sikkhaṁ paccācikkhāmi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.27
Pali: Kinnumāva samaṇiyo yā samaṇiyo sakyadhītaro. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.28
Pali: Santaññāpi samaṇiyo lajjiniyo kukkuccikā sikkhākāmā, tāsāhaṁ santike brahmacariyaṁ carissāmī’ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.29
Pali: Abhiramāyye, svākkhāto dhammo; 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.30
Pali: cara brahmacariyaṁ sammā dukkhassa antakiriyāyā”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.31
Pali: Dutiyampi vattabbā. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.32
Pali: Tatiyampi vattabbā. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.33
Pali: Sace paṭinissajjati iccetaṁ kusalaṁ, 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.34
Pali: no ce paṭinissajjati āpatti dukkaṭassa. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.35
Pali: Sā bhikkhunī samanubhāsitabbā. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.36
Pali: Evañca pana, bhikkhave, samanubhāsitabbā. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.37
Pali: Byattāya bhikkhuniyā paṭibalāya saṅgho ñāpetabbo—

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.38
Pali: “Suṇātu me, ayye, saṅgho. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.39
Pali: Ayaṁ itthannāmā bhikkhunī kupitā anattamanā evaṁ vadeti—

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.40
Pali: ‘buddhaṁ paccācikkhāmi, dhammaṁ paccācikkhāmi, saṅghaṁ paccācikkhāmi, sikkhaṁ paccācikkhāmi. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.41
Pali: Kinnumāva samaṇiyo yā samaṇiyo sakyadhītaro. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.42
Pali: Santaññāpi samaṇiyo lajjiniyo kukkuccikā sikkhākāmā tāsāhaṁ santike brahmacariyaṁ carissāmī’ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.43
Pali: Sā taṁ vatthuṁ na paṭinissajjati. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.44
Pali: Yadi saṅghassa pattakallaṁ, saṅgho itthannāmaṁ bhikkhuniṁ samanubhāseyya tassa vatthussa paṭinissaggāya. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.45
Pali: Esā ñatti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.46
Pali: Suṇātu me, ayye, saṅgho. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.47

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.53

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.54
Pali: yassā nakkhamati sā, bhāseyya. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.55
Pali: Dutiyampi etamatthaṁ vadāmi …pe… 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.56

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.57

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.58
Pali: Khamati saṅghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṁ dhārayāmī”ti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.59

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.60
Pali: Dvīhi kammavācāhi thullaccayā. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.61
Pali: Kammavācāpariyosāne āpatti saṅghādisesassa. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.62
Pali: Saṅghādisesaṁ ajjhāpajjantiyā ñattiyā dukkaṭaṁ, dvīhi kammavācāhi thullaccayā paṭippassambhanti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.63
Pali: Ayampīti 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.64
Pali: purimāyo upādāya vuccati. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.65

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.66

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.67

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.68
Pali: saṅghamhā nissārīyati. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.69
Pali: Saṅghādisesoti 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.1.70
Pali: …pe… tenapi vuccati saṅghādisesoti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.2.1

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.2.6

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.3.5
Pali: ādikammikāyāti. 

pli-tv-bi-vb-ss10:2.3.6
Pali: Sattamasaṅghādisesasikkhāpadaṁ niṭṭhitaṁ.

Pali: Aṭṭhamasaṅghādisesasikkhāpadaṁ niṭṭhitaṁ.
